<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">новина́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">noviná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новинка.html>нови́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">novínka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новинка.html>нови́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новинка.html>нови́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новинка.html>нови́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>novelty
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:новинка.html>нови́нку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>novínku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">new <i>(to)</i>; something of a novelty</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>new product, new arrival</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nóvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">god</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ний</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, based on <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>год</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Nóvyj god</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">New Year</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новодевичий.html>новоде́вичий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">novodévičij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Novodevichy <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">referring to various locations named as such, e.g. <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Novodevichy_Convent" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Novodevichy Convent">Novodevichy Convent</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Novodevichy_Cemetery" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Novodevichy Cemetery">Novodevichy Cemetery</a>; the name originally referred to the convent, and literally means "New Maidens'"</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nóvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новость.html>но́вость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nóvostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новость.html>но́вости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новость.html>но́вости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новость.html>новосте́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>novelty</li>
<li>news
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:срочный.html>сро́чная</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:новость.html>но́вость</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sróčnaja <b>nóvostʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">newsflash</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:преподнести.html>преподнести́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприятный.html>неприя́тную</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:новость.html>но́вость</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prepodnestí neprijátnuju <b>nóvostʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to communicate/bring bad news</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***новый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вый</a> (115)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*nòvъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*néwos</i> whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">new</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">novel</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nóvyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)нове́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:новь.html>нове́й</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новейший.html>нове́йший</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>new</li>
<li>novel</li>
<li>recent</li>
<li>modern</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:новь.html>новь</a> (31440)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nóvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новь.html>новь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">novʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новь.html>но́ви</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новь.html>но́ви</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:новь.html>но́вей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">high style</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> newness, novelty, something new in people's lives</li>
<li>unplowed land, virgin land</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">regional</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> grain from a new harvest</li></ol>

***нога.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́</a> (128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*noga</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₃nogʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">claw, nail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">nail</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ungulate</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">nagas</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">ناخن</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nâxon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">unguis</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es">uña</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Welsh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Welsh language">Welsh</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cy">ewin</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nogá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ноги́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>но́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ног</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>leg
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>встать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>ноги</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vstatʹ ná <b>nogi</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to recover from illness; become independent financially and economically</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***ножницы.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ножницы.html>но́жницы</a> (8505)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нож.html>нож</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nož</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ножницы.html>но́жницы</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nóžnicy</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> <abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ножницы.html>но́жниц</a></b>, <i>plural only</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>scissors, shears, clipper, cutter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:механический.html>механи́ческие</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ножницы.html>но́жницы</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mexaníčeskije <b>nóžnicy</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">alligator shears</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">гильоти́нные <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ножницы.html>но́жницы</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gilʹotínnyje <b>nóžnicy</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">guillotine shears</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ножницы.html>но́жницы</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ноготь.html>ногте́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nóžnicy</b> dlja nogtéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nail clippers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садовый.html>садо́вые</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ножницы.html>но́жницы</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sadóvyje <b>nóžnicy</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">cutters</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">economics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> disproportion, discrepancy</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ножной.html>ножно́й</a> (28236)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nogá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ножной.html>ножно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nožnój</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> foot, leg
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ножной.html>ножна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ванна.html>ва́нна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nožnája</b> vánna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">footbath</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ножной.html>ножны́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мускул.html>му́скулы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nožnýje</b> múskuly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">leg muscles</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>foot-powered
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ножной.html>ножна́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:швейный.html>шве́йная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nožnája</b> švéjnaja mašínka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">foot-powered sewing machine</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ноль.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>ноль</a> (3527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>ноль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nolʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>нуля́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>нули́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>нуле́й</a></b>) <i>or</i> <br />
<strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>ноль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nolʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>ноля́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>ноли́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>ноле́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>zero (0)
<dl><dd><ul><li>Next number: <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (1)</li></ul></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:абсолютный.html>абсолю́тный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>ноль</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">absoljútnyj <b>nolʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">absolute zero</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>nil, nothing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выиграть.html>вы́играть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:счет.html>счётом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>ноль</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">výigratʹ so sčótom tri <b>nolʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to win three to nothing</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>precisely, exactly <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">time</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двенадцать.html>двена́дцать</a> ноль-но́ль</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v dvenádcatʹ nolʹ-nólʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">at twelve sharp</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cipher, nobody, nonentity, a paltry person
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полный.html>по́лный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>ноль</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:математика.html>матема́тике</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on pólnyj <b>nolʹ</b> v matemátike</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he’s terrible in mathematics</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>ноль</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:палочка.html>па́лочки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nolʹ</b> bez páločki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a complete nonentity</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">zero without a line</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:круглый.html>кру́глый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>ноль</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krúglyj <b>nolʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">a complete nonentity</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">a round zero</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> nothing, naught
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стричь.html>стричь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>ноль</a></b></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stričʹ pod <b>nolʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cut off all the hair</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>ноль</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:внимание.html>внима́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná na nevó <b>nolʹ</b> vnimánija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">she pays him no heed</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***номер.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:номер.html>но́мер</a> (495)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:номер.html>но́мер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nómer</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:номер.html>но́мера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:номер.html>номера́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:номер.html>номеро́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>ordinal number</li>
<li>size (of clothes or shoes)</li>
<li>room (in a hotel)</li>
<li>number, issue (e.g. of a magazine or a newspaper)</li>
<li>item, turn, trick (e.g., in a circus)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Frequently abbreviated to <span class="Latn" lang="ru">№</span>. Doubling indicates plural: <span class="Latn" lang="ru">№№</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:номер.html>номера</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nomera</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
